si khron zhing chen khongs dkar mdzes bod rigs rang skyong khul gyi nub byang ngos dang 'bri chu'i shar 'gram na yod pa'i rdzong zhig rdzong mi dmangs srid gzhung de ni dgon chen na yod /

... bsdus pa'i sdom /
mang po nas btus te phyogs gcig tu bsgrigs pa'i sdom /
... bsdus pa'i sdom gyi tshigs su bcad pa /
tshig don mang po phyogs gcig tu bsdus pa'i sdom tshig tshigs bcad du bsgrigs pa /
... bsdus pa'i dpe /
dpe'i rgyan gyi nang gses shig ste /
dpe can don dang /
dpe gnyis khyad chos gcig tsam min par mtshungs chos gzhan gyis kyang 'dra bar bsdus pa'i rgyan zhig ... bsdus pa'i gzugs can /
gzugs can gyi rgyan gyi nang gses shig ste /
dpe can don gyi khyad gzhi khyad chos 'ga' zhig dpe'i khyad gzhi  khyad chos dang ngo bo dbyer med du bkod cing /
bar gyi 'brel sgra bsdus pa'i rgyan zhig ... bsdus po /
rgyas po ma yin pa /
...gsol tshigs bsdus po /
...bsdus bris /
... bsdus 'bring /
bsdus grwa'i rigs lam 'bring ba ste /
drug sgra rtsi tshul /
dgag gzhi rtsi tshul /
dris 'phangs kyi rnam gzhag sogs dbang po 'bring ba rnams kyis slob rgyu'i bsdus tshan rnams so /
... bsdus tshan /
bsdus gzhung nang gi tshan pa la zer /
dper na /
kha dog dkar dmar zer ba bsdus tshan gcig yin log min log ces pa bsdus tshan gcig rgyu 'bras chung ba zhes pa bsdus tshan gcig byas pa lta bu /
... bsdus gzhung /
gtan tshig rig pa dang mtshan nyid rigs lam slob pa'i dpe deb /
... bsdus gzhom /
bsdus 'joms dang don gcig bsdus yig bskungs yig ste /
tsheg khyim gcig tu ming gnyis gsum tsam bsdus pa'i yi ge dper na /
s+r+g+yas /
'khaur sogs /
...s+r+g+yas...'khaur... bsdus ra /
bsdus grwa ste mtshan nyid rigs lam gyi thog mar slob pa'i gzhung zhig ... bsdus shing ma bsdus pa'i gzugs can /
gzugs can gyi rgyan gyi nang gses shig ste /
dpe can don gyi khyad gzhi khyad chos 'ga' zhig dpe'i khyad gzhi khyad chos kyi gzugs su bkod cing /
bar gyi 'brel sgra 'ga' zhig bsdus la /
'ga' zhig ma bsdus pa'i rgyan zhig ... bsdeb pa /
sdeb pa'i ma 'ongs pa /
bsdebs pa /
sdeb pa'i 'das pa /
bsdebs 'dzogs /
yul sdeb 'phung thebs pa /
...khang chung gcig gi nang du ca lag mang po bsdebs 'dzogs thebs 'dug ... bsdo ba /
sdo ba'i ma 'ongs pa /
bsdog chas /
bsdog rgyu'i yo byad /
...dngos po bsdog chas brgyab nas phyogs la thon pa /
... bsdog pa /
.sdog pa'i ma 'ongs pa /
.rnying bshams pa /
... ko lham soT kyi lhan pa /
... bsdogs pa /
sdog pa'i 'das pa /
bsdong ba /
sdong ba'i ma 'ongs pa /
bsdongs pa /
sdong ba'i 'das pa /
bsdom pa /
sdud pa'i don du go ba'i sdom pa'i ma 'ongs pa /
bsdoms grangs /
khyon 'bor bsdoms pa'i grangs ka /
... bsdoms pa /
sdud pa'i don du go ba'i sdom pa'i 'das pa /
bsdoms 'bor /
khyon bsdoms kyi mang nyung /
...gong gsal rtsis grangs kyi bsdoms 'bor gzhir bzhag nas gsham du cha 'grems byed dgos /
... bsdoms rtsis /
gcig tu bsdoms pa'i rtsis /
... bsdoms tshig gzhug bsdoms brgyab pa'i brjod tshig ... bsdos /
rnying tshur rgol byas pa /
... bsdos pa /
sdo ba'i 'das pa /
